<div class="mds-area-pf1"><div class="cnt_well_c1 section"><div class="mod modCnt_well_1 mds-cmp-content20">

	<div class="pf1a_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c1 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_1 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_1">
	
	<h1 class="hl ">
						THE 2013 CHEVROLET SONIC HATCHBACK FEATURING THE ALL-NEW SONIC RS</h1>	
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						</div>
				</div>
</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>  We designed Sonic to be truly a car for firsts, and through this go-getter spirit it became the first and only car in its class with 10 standard air <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_2" class="ln disclaimer_1">bags<sup>†</sup></a>,<sup><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_16" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a></sup> and the only car in its class with an available turbocharged engine – offering up to 40 MPG <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_1" class="ln disclaimer_1">highway<sup>†</sup></a>. With all that power under the hood, it’s the most fun-to-drive car. As the first car to skydive, kickflip and star in a music video, Sonic is ready to take on whatever gets your blood pumping. It was built for people who try new things, seek discovery and live life to the fullest.</p>
<p>  </p>
<p>  To stay connected while you’re out and about, Sonic is ready to keep your tech-savvy fingers limbered up. Equipped with available Chevrolet <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_19" class="ln disclaimer_1">MyLink<sup>†</sup></a> Radio and a 7-inch diagonal color touch-screen, you can access you phone, your friends and the rest of the world at the touch of your fingertips. Ushering in a world of excitement, Sonic invites everyone to experience their own firsts with three words: Let’s do this!</p>
<p>  </p>
<p><a href="/sonic-hatchback-car/videos.html" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'grid-1col'});}">Check out these videos to learn more about the RS</a></p>

	</div>
</li><li><div class="parbase download section"><a class="dl_pdf" href="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Ownership/Manuals%20and%20Videos/02_pdf/MY2013%20Sonic%20Spec%20Sheet%20R1_web%20(1).pdf" target="_blank" id="" title="Download Spec Sheet">Download Spec Sheet</a>
	</div>
</li></ul></div>

	<div class="parsys_cnt_well_1 parsys_c1"><div class="grid_col2_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf2">
	<div class="pf2a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					The Best of the Best</h2>
			<h3 class="pt">
					Introducing the all-new RS Hatchback</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Say hello to the newest Sonic model. Amped up from the inside out, the RS is begging<br>
you to hit the road and never look back. As you hit the accelerator, you get immediate<br>
satisfaction with a standard turbocharged engine and unique sporty gear ratios. Complemented perfectly by a lowered and stiffened suspension with performance-tuned<br>
dampers, the RS gives you incredible control, creating the ultimate Sonic driving experience.</p>
<p>Get your adrenaline going as you slide into heated, leather-appointed front bucket<br>
seats with sueded microfiber inserts and grab hold of the leather-wrapped sport<br>
steering wheel with racing-inspired flat-bottom design. The ultimate Sonic<br>
experience is enhanced by an interior that is upgraded with unique center stack<br>
trim and contrasting red stitching throughout. Enhanced from the ground up,<br>
the RS gives Sonic an overall impressive balance of savvy and power.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p></div>
				</div></div>

<div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_top">
			<div class="inner" style="width: 482px; top: 110px; margin-bottom: 110px; margin-left: 0px;">
			  <h3 class="pt"
				>
				Uncompromised Control</h3>
		<div class="tx">
				<p>                    RS is the perfect blend of beauty and beast. Amplifying the rush from the turbocharged engine is responsive handling to match. The new suspension is designed to add control that perfectly harnesses the power of the engine. You’ll feel it hug the road around every bend and curve. So whether it’s a winding drive down the coast or just switching lanes in rush hour, you’ll feel comfortable knowing Sonic will respond to your hands around the leather-wrapped sport steering wheel exactly how you want it to. </p></div>
		</div>

<div class="grid_col2_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf2">
	<div class="pf2a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			It’s got the look</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Sonic is the only small car built in the United <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_6" class="ln disclaimer_1">States<sup>†</sup></a> and packs a whole lot of attitude. You can see it from its chiseled front end to the rear spoiler. Even the rear door handles are hidden to keep that sporty, clean look without sacrificing functionality. Its aggressive stance, dynamic lines and expressive wheel arches let people know that Sonic is ready for some fun. When you have a car with this much power under the hood and up to 40 MPG <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_1" class="ln disclaimer_1">highway<sup>†</sup></a>, it has to be backed up by a look to match.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf2b">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2b_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Get noticed</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Sonic is going to catch an eye or two. Its defined front end with exposed headlamps, unique dual-port grille and motorcycle-inspired rear taillamps make a strong visual statement. Kick it up a notch with foglamps and chrome accents standard on LTZ and RS, and rest assured you’ll make an all-eyes-on-you entrance long before you even arrive.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p></div>
		</div>
</div>

	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_top">
			<div class="inner" style="width: 320px; top: 80px; margin-bottom: 80px; margin-left: -30px;">
			  <h3 class="pt"
				style="color: #FFFFFF">
				Pick your wheels</h3>
		<div class="tx" style="color: #FFFFFF">
				<p>Boost its aggressive and sporty stance with eye-catching wheel options. From the LS steel wheels with full bolt-on wheel covers      to the whole lineup of available dealer-installed Z-Spec wheels, your Sonic will be riding in style. The LT sports 15&quot; painted aluminum wheels, or you can upgrade to the optional 16&quot; wheels available with the Wheels and Foglamp Package. For a little more edge to your ride, go for the LTZ model with standard 17&quot; painted aluminum wheels. The RS tops off its impressive upgrades with 17&quot; Midnight Silver aluminum wheels.</p></div>

<div class="grid_col3_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf3a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Prepare for takeoff</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Sonic was recently named one of <em>Ward’s</em> Top 10 Interiors. Joining the ranks of Audi, Land Rover and Infiniti, the dual cockpit interior and motorcycle-inspired instrument cluster with silver accents get your blood pumping before you even turn the key. The performance-inspired design elements Sonic boasts on the exterior are exactly what you find when you get behind the wheel. Sonic is ready to be driven, so grab onto its 3-spoke steering wheel designed for optimal grip and hold on tight.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3b">
		<div class="pf3b_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Comfort and convenience</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Sure, Sonic has an edge, but it’s made for comfort too. Every seat in Sonic was designed to give you and your passengers the best ride possible. Enjoy perforated leatherette seats in the LTZ, or leather-appointed seats with sueded microfiber inserts in the Sonic RS. Both models provide added comfort for you and your front seat passenger with heated seats. And rest assured, Sonic has your back with OnStar<sup>®</sup> Turn-by-Turn <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_3" class="ln disclaimer_1">Navigation<sup>†</sup></a>, standard for the first six months. With the press of a button, you’ll be connected with a friendly OnStar<sup>®</sup> Advisor ready to help get you where you’re going. So buckle up and get ready to go.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="pf3c_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Go ahead and load it up</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                    That hatchback is good for more than just a sporty look. Sonic Hatchback offers ample cargo space and many ways to get it. Seating for five with 19 cubic feet of cargo <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_7" class="ln disclaimer_1">space<sup>†</sup></a> will bring your friends and everything you need. With its 60/40 split-folding rear seat and up to 47.7 cubic feet with the rear seats folded down, you’ll be able to find a configuration that’s just right, whether it’s heading to the beach or grabbing groceries after work. Sonic even gives you unique storage solutions for everything you want to keep within reach, including upper and lower glove boxes. Bringing a water bottle with you? There are holders incorporated right into the front doors. There’s a smart way to make use of space, and the Sonic Hatchback is brilliant. </p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

</div><div class="mds-area-pf1"><div class="cnt_well_c1 section"><div class="mod modCnt_well_1 mds-cmp-content20" id="Performance">
	<div class="parsys_cnt_well_1 parsys_c1"><div class="section grid_col1_c1"><div class="mds-area-pf1">
	<div class="pf1a_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					Unmatched Performance</h2>
			</div></div>
<div class="grid_col3_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf3a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			The only turbocharged engine available in<br/> its class</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Be forewarned: After you take your friends for a ride, they may begin to show signs of Sonic envy — because when you turbocharge the drive, things get a lot more interesting. Sonic achieved 0-60 mph in less than 8 <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_20" class="ln disclaimer_1">seconds<sup>†</sup></a> on the test track. Whether it’s heading out for a quick skate session, driving up a mountain for a morning hike or just merging onto the freeway, Sonic LT, LTZ and RS models offer the available power you need. With 138 horsepower and 148 lb.-ft. of the most available torque in its class, you’ll soon find out that Sonic is the most fun-to-drive car and it offers up to 40 MPG <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_1" class="ln disclaimer_1">hwy<sup>†</sup></a>.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3b">
		<div class="pf3b_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Handling and a comfortable ride, together<br/> at last</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Sonic engineers went through hundreds of suspension variations until they found the perfect blend of handling and a comfortable ride, giving Sonic extraordinary agility and sportiness. Its standard ECOTEC 1.8L I-4 engine with 5-speed manual transmission puts the control of driving back in your hands. With 138 horsepower and 125 lb.-ft. of torque, Sonic knows how to take care of business.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="pf3c_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Designed with you in mind</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                    No matter how you slice it, Sonic offers options that will get you excited to hit the road. Sonic offers Hill Start Assist, which helps you stay put on steep inclines while you transition from the brake pedal to the gas pedal. Whether it's going downhill in reverse or driving uphill, Sonic keeps you steady. </p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

</div><div class="mds-area-pf1"><div class="cnt_well_c1 section"><div class="mod modCnt_well_1 mds-cmp-content20" id="Efficiency">
	<div class="parsys_cnt_well_1 parsys_c1"><div class="grid_col1plus2_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pn3a"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					An Eye on Fuel Economy</h2>
			<h3 class="pt">
					40 MPG <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_1" class="ln disclaimer_1">hwy<sup>†</sup></a> — so many miles, so little gas</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Whether you’re commuting during the week or taking a long road trip on the weekend, Sonic, equipped with the available turbocharged engine on LT and LTZ, offers up to 488 highway <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_18" class="ln disclaimer_1">miles<sup>†</sup></a> on a single tank of gas. Engineering technology in performance and design makes it possible. The available 1.4L turbocharged engine offers up to 40 MPG on the <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_1" class="ln disclaimer_1">highway<sup>†</sup></a> without sacrificing its power and athleticism. There’s a lot that goes into making a car as fuel efficient as possible, which translates into money in your pocket — not the pump.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p></div>
				</div></div>
</div>

<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Stay in the loop while out and about</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                    Sonic keeps you connected to your friends and entertainment on the go. Sonic offers extensive technology features like available Chevrolet MyLink Radio, standard Bluetooth<sup>®</sup> wireless technology for select <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_4" class="ln disclaimer_1">phones<sup>†</sup></a> that allows you to take calls while keeping your hands on the wheel, or OnStar<sup>®</sup> Turn-by-Turn Navigation, standard for six <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_3" class="ln disclaimer_1">months<sup>†</sup></a>. And with the available USB <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_8" class="ln disclaimer_1">port<sup>†</sup></a> to plug in your musical gadgets and SiriusXM Satellite Radio with a 3-month <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_9" class="ln disclaimer_1">trial<sup>†</sup>,</a> you get the music and entertainment you want, when you want it. </p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div></div>
<div class="grid_col3_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf3a_parsys"><div class="parbase cnt_imgpar_c1 section"><div class="mds-cmp-content01 cnt_mmpar_1  mod modCnt_mmpar_1 ">
	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<h3 class="pt">
						<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared Resources/01_images/final_icons_4C_mylink.png" alt="" width="92" height="32" class="img"/><span>
									Chevrolet MyLink Radio</span>
							</h3>
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>The available Chevrolet <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_19" class="ln disclaimer_1">MyLink<sup>†</sup></a> Radio starts with a 7-inch diagonal full-color display that lets you stay in touch in style. A touch screen menu connects you to everything you need and, when the vehicle is stopped, allows you to project video and even personal photo albums onto the screen from your phone. Connect your compatible smartphone wirelessly via Bluetooth<sup>®</sup> and listen to music, get directions or make phone calls all with the touch of a fingertip.</p>
<p><a href="/mylink-bring-your-own-media.html" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'grid-3col'});}">Learn more about MyLink.<br>
</a></p>
<p></p></div>
				</div>
		</div></div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3b">
		<div class="pf3b_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_imgpar_c1 section"><div class="mds-cmp-content01 cnt_mmpar_1  mod modCnt_mmpar_1 ">
	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<h3 class="pt">
						<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared Resources/01_images/final_icons_4C_bluetooth.png" alt="" width="127" height="32" class="img"/><span>
									Wireless technology</span>
							</h3>
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Take calls without ever taking your hands off the steering wheel through the connectivity of standard <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_4" class="ln disclaimer_1">Bluetooth<sup>®†</sup></a> wireless technology for select phones and steering wheel-mounted controls. Bluetooth connectivity for your phone is standard on every model. Bluetooth audio streaming is included with the Chevrolet <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_19" class="ln disclaimer_1">MyLink<sup>†</sup></a> Radio. You can also connect your iPod, MP3 player or music-loaded flash drive into the auxiliary input jack or available USB <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_8" class="ln disclaimer_1">port<sup>†</sup></a> for a direct line to the radio.</p></div>
				</div>
		</div></div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="pf3c_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_imgpar_c1 section"><div class="mds-cmp-content01 cnt_mmpar_1  mod modCnt_mmpar_1 ">
	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<h3 class="pt">
						<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared Resources/01_images/final_icons_1C_mobile_app.png" alt="" width="32" height="32" class="img"/><span>
									Mobile apps</span>
							</h3>
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Sonic keeps you in the loop with the myChevrolet mobile <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_5" class="ln disclaimer_1">app<sup>†</sup></a> with the connectivity of OnStar <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_10" class="ln disclaimer_1">RemoteLink™<sup>†</sup></a>. With this app, you can remotely lock or unlock your vehicle in case you get locked out at the lake, check vehicle diagnostics such as oil life and tire <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_14" class="ln disclaimer_1">pressure<sup>†</sup></a> or even remotely start it when equipped with available remote vehicle starter <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_15" class="ln disclaimer_1">system<sup>†</sup></a>. And you’ll never get lost in a parking lot with a real map reminder. Want to schedule a service appointment? It’s done in a click. And should you ever need help, roadside assistance is there 24/7. Available from the <a href="http://itunes.apple.com/us/app/mychevrolet/id398596699?mt=8" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://itunes.apple.com/us/app/mychevrolet/id398596699?mt=8');" target="_blank">iTunes Store</a> and <a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.gm.chevrolet.nomad.ownership&feature=more_from_developer" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.gm.chevrolet.nomad.ownership&feature=more_from_developer');" target="_blank">Google Play</a>.</p></div>
				</div>
		</div></div>
</div>

	<div class="pf3a">

	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<h3 class="pt">
						<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared Resources/01_images/final_icons_4C_siriusxm.png" alt="" width="92" height="32" class="img"/><span>
									The sounds of Sonic</span>
							</h3>
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>                  In Sonic, you can listen to commercial-free programs through the three-month trial of SiriusXM Satellite <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_9" class="ln disclaimer_1">Radio<sup>†</sup></a>. Or, stream your favorite audio services, like Pandora<sup>® </sup>Internet Radio and Stitcher <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_5" class="ln disclaimer_1">SmartRadio™<sup>†</sup></a><sup>,<a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_11" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a></sup> or your own music library, from your compatible smartphone through its available <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_4" class="ln disclaimer_1">Bluetooth<sup>†</sup></a> audio streaming feature for select phones. Just download the <a href="http://www.pandora.com/" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://www.pandora.com/');" target="_blank">Pandora Internet Radio</a> or <a href="http://www.stitcher.com/" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://www.stitcher.com/');" target="_blank">Stitcher SmartRadio</a> app to your mobile device.</p></div>

</div>
	<div class="pf3b">
		<div class="pf3b_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_imgpar_c1 section"><div class="mds-cmp-content01 cnt_mmpar_1  mod modCnt_mmpar_1 ">
	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<h3 class="pt">
						<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared Resources/01_images/final_icons_1C_navigation_system.png" alt="" width="32" height="32" class="img"/><span>
									OnStar Turn-by-Turn Navigation</span>
							</h3>
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Being lost will be a thing of the past with Sonic. It includes the <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_3" class="ln disclaimer_1">OnStar<sup>®†</sup></a> Directions &amp; Connections Plan<sup>®</sup> with Turn-by-Turn Navigation, standard for the first six months. One press of the blue button and you are connected to an Advisor who can help you get to your destination anytime. Voice-guided directions can even be downloaded right into your car. You can even plan ahead with OnStar eNav℠, which lets you send destinations from MapQuest.com<sup>®</sup> to your car. Call them up anytime with a simple voice command.</p></div>
				</div>
		</div></div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="pf3c_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_imgpar_c1 section"><div class="mds-cmp-content01 cnt_mmpar_1  mod modCnt_mmpar_1 ">
	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<h3 class="pt">
						<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared Resources/01_images/final_icons_1C_remote_start.png" alt="" width="32" height="32" class="img"/><span>
									Start it up using your phone</span>
							</h3>
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Attention to detail is what turns a good experience into a great experience. That’s why Sonic offers available remote start <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_15" class="ln disclaimer_1">capability<sup>†</sup></a>, so you can start your Sonic before you even open the door. It means in the dead of winter, you can let your car warm up without having to brave the cold, or in the height of summer let it cool down before you get in the driver’s seat. It’s just another way Sonic keeps your comfort in mind. Even better, the OnStar RemoteLink mobile <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_10" class="ln disclaimer_1">app<sup>†</sup></a> allows you to start your vehicle and lock or unlock the doors from anywhere you have cell service if your vehicle is equipped with remote <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_15" class="ln disclaimer_1">start<sup>†</sup></a>.</p>
<p></p></div>
				</div>
		</div></div>
</div>
</div>

	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					A HIGH-TECH MOBILE TRIO</h2>
			</div></div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			BringGo</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>The <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_24" class="ln disclaimer_1">BringGo<sup>†</sup></a> navigation <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_29" class="ln disclaimer_1">app<sup>†</sup></a> offers plenty of easy-to-use features that let you revel in the fun of discovering new destinations without the stress of getting lost. Explore with the convenience of 3-D maps with lane suggestions, live traffic data, local search via Google™, a Where Am I? Locator and other features that help you stay in the loop. Read More.<br>
</p>
<p>Purchase it now from the <a href="https://itunes.apple.com/us/app/bringgo-usa-can/id539430347?mt=8&ign-mpt=uo%3D2" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('https://itunes.apple.com/us/app/bringgo-usa-can/id539430347?mt=8&ign-mpt=uo%3D2');" target="_blank">App Store</a> or <a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=gogo3.ennavcore2&feature=search_result#?t=W251bGwsMSwxLDEsImdvZ28zLmVubmF2Y29yZTIiXQ" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=gogo3.ennavcore2&feature=search_result#?t=W251bGwsMSwxLDEsImdvZ28zLmVubmF2Y29yZTIiXQ');" target="_blank">Google Play</a>.</p></div>
		</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Siri Eyes Free</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Chevrolet is the first vehicle manufacturer to offer <a href="http://www.apple.com/ios/siri/siri-faq/" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://www.apple.com/ios/siri/siri-faq/');" target="_blank">Siri Eyes Free</a><sup><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_30" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a></sup> to <a href="http://www.apple.com/ios/siri/siri-faq/" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://www.apple.com/ios/siri/siri-faq/');" target="_blank">iPhone</a> users. <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_29" class="ln disclaimer_1">Siri<sup>†</sup></a> lets you take charge with your hands on the wheel and your eyes on the road. Complete an array of hands-free tasks like composing text and email messages to stored contacts on your phone by directing Siri through voice command. Simply connect your iPhone 4S or iPhone 5 with available <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_31" class="ln disclaimer_1">Chevrolet MyLink<sup>†</sup></a> via <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_4" class="ln disclaimer_1">Bluetooth<sup>†</sup></a>, then use the steering wheel voice activation button to begin.</p></div>
		</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			TuneIn</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Experience a new level of entertainment on the go with access to over 70,000 radio stations from around the world. Just download the free <a href="http://www.tunein.com" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://www.tunein.com');" target="_blank">TuneIn</a><sup><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_29" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a></sup> app to your compatible smartphone and connect it to available <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_31" class="ln disclaimer_1">Chevrolet MyLink<sup>†</sup></a>. Then sit back and enjoy a selection of live, local, international and Internet radio from every corner of the globe.</p>
<p>Download it now from the <a href="https://itunes.apple.com/us/app/tunein-radio-listen-to-live/id418987775?mt=8" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('https://itunes.apple.com/us/app/tunein-radio-listen-to-live/id418987775?mt=8');" target="_blank">App Store</a> or <a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=tunein.player&feature=search_result#?t=W251bGwsMSwxLDEsInR1bmVpbi5wbGF5ZXIiXQ" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=tunein.player&feature=search_result#?t=W251bGwsMSwxLDEsInR1bmVpbi5wbGF5ZXIiXQ');" target="_blank">Google Play</a>.</p></div>

	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					Make It Feel Like Home</h2>
			<h3 class="pt">
					Accessorize it to Make it as Unique as You are</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Celebrate being unique by customizing your Sonic. From body graphics to functional accessories, you can make your Sonic as much a part of who you are as you make your home. With a variety of available <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_13" class="ln disclaimer_1">graphics<sup>†</sup></a>, you’ll find a style that matches your personality on the move. Standing still you’ll look sharp too, with dealer-installed white or black wheels that complement your graphics. Inside, you can add dealer-installed Chevy Accessories like available doorsill plates to give stepping in a stepped-up look. Finally, hit the gas in super style with an available Sport Pedal Kit featuring brushed aluminum covers with rubber grips. Be the first in your crew to put your spin on Sonic. Start your customization at <a href="http://www.gmaccessorieszone.com/Chevrolet/en-US/Sonic/2012" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://www.gmaccessorieszone.com/Chevrolet/en-US/Sonic/2012');" target="_blank">Chevrolet Accessories.</a></p></div>

	<div class="txtWrp">The 2013 Sonic LTZ shown with dealer-installed Z-Spec appearance <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_27" class="ln disclaimer_1">accessories<sup>†</sup></a> and graphic <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_28" class="ln disclaimer_1">wrap<sup>†</sup></a>.</div>
						</figcaption>
		   	    	</figure>	
	</div>

				<li class="mm_mos_1_item" id="">

</div><div class="mds-area-pf1"><div class="cnt_well_c1 section"><div class="mod modCnt_well_1 mds-cmp-content20" id="Safety">
	<div class="parsys_cnt_well_1 parsys_c1"><div class="grid_col1plus2_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pn3a"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					Safety</h2>
			<h3 class="pt">
					A safety philosophy that runs deep</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Sonic boasts aggressive styling and impressive power, but make no mistake ­— with Sonic, safety is a priority. Sonic is the first and only car in is class to receive a 5-Star Overall Vehicle Score for safety from NHTSA and was also named a Top Safety Pick by the Insurance Institute for Highway Safety (IIHS).</p>
<p>Sonic is built around a steel safety cage and offers extensive safety features for prevention, reaction and response technology to optimize safety before, during and after a crash, if needed. &nbsp;Other advancements you can count on — including daytime running lamps and a Tire Pressure Monitoring <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_14" class="ln disclaimer_1">System<sup>†</sup></a> — are just a few of the ways we help you avoid trouble on the road.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p></div>
				</div></div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3bc">
		<div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2013%20Sonic%20Hatchback/Model%20Overview/01_images/2013-Sonic-Hatch-Safety-cnt-well-1-648X347-01.jpg" alt="" width="648" height="347" class="mm"/></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="grid_col3_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf3a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Prevent</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>From the moment you set out on the road, technologies like the StabiliTrak<sup>®</sup> Electronic Stability Control System with traction control are at the ready. On slippery surfaces, StabiliTrak helps you stay on course by detecting the difference between the path being steered and the direction the vehicle is actually traveling.</p>
<p>It then uses the brakes and, if necessary, adjusts engine torque to help you keep your Sonic on track. What’s more, 4-wheel antilock brakes help maintain control and stability during hard braking by preventing wheel lockup. And Electronic Brake Force Distribution on the front and rear brakes has Panic Brake Assist to help optimize stopping power.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3b">
		<div class="pf3b_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Protect</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Sometimes, however, trouble finds you. And if a moderate-to-severe collision does occur, Sonic is designed to respond quickly as the first and only car in its <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_16" class="ln disclaimer_1">class<sup>†</sup></a> with 10 standard air <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_2" class="ln disclaimer_1">bags<sup>†</sup></a>.Sensors throughout the vehicle determine how many air bags deploy — including knee air bags for the driver and front passenger. Adding to this protection, the cabin is reinforced with high-strength steel throughout. Meanwhile, front and rear “crush zones” are designed to compress in a controlled manner, helping absorb and channel energy away from the cabin. But our protective measures don’t end there.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="pf3c_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Respond</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>In many crashes, built-in sensors can automatically alert an <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_3" class="ln disclaimer_1">OnStar<sup>®†</sup></a> Advisor, who is immediately connected into the vehicle to see if you need help. Even if you don’t respond, the Advisor can use GPS technology to pinpoint your exact location and request that emergency help be sent right away. It’s part of the <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-sonic-hatchback_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_3" class="ln disclaimer_1">OnStar<sup>†</sup></a> Directions &amp; Connections<sup>®</sup> Plan, which is standard for the first six months, because nothing is more important than your safety.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="parsys_cnt_well_2 parsys_list_c1"><ul class="ull ui-layout-horizontal ui-layout-right"><li><div class="share parbase share_c2 section"><div class="mod modShare_2">

	<div class="parsys_cnt_well_1 parsys_c1"><div class="grid_col1plus2_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pn3a"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					How Sustainable is the Sonic?</h2>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Check out its “Ecologic” Features. Here at Chevrolet, we believe in being a responsible steward of our environment. Recently, we’ve developed a new way to communicate some of the environmentally significant features of each vehicle we make. We call it “Ecologic.”</p></div>
				</div></div>
<div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05">
			<div class="inner">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared%20Resources/ecologic/2013-chevrolet-model-overview-ecologic-cnt-well-1-308x76-01.jpg" alt="" width="308" height="76" class="mm"/></div>


</div>
</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Every aspect of Ecologic is audited by Two Tomorrows, an  independent third party sustainability auditor. To learn more about  Ecologic and the Two Tomorrows’ process, click here.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3bc">
		<div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared%20Resources/ecologic/2013-chevrolet-model-overview-ecologic-cnt-well-1-648x315-02.jpg" alt="" width="648" height="315" class="mm"/></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="grid_col2_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf2">
	<div class="pf2a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Fuel-Saving Technologies</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Continuously Variable Valve Timing (VVT) adjusts airflow in and out of the combustion chamber under all engine speeds, which makes for better fuel economy and lower emissions. Electric power steering uses an electric motor instead of an engine-driven belt, which results in a lighter overall workload and better fuel economy.</p>
<p></p>
<p>The engine has been factory-filled with engine oil meeting GM’s new dexosTM specification, which has improved viscosity characteristics as compared to the previous GF-4 oil, contributing to better fuel economy. An available advanced small-displacement 1.4-liter turbocharged Ecotec four-cylinder engine offers 40 MPG highway. With reduced engine displacement and an advanced turbocharger, this vehicle delivers segment-leading fuel economy and torque.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf2b">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2b_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Responsible Manufacturing</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                    Landfill gas supplies more than 20% of the total energy for heating and cooling of the final assembly facility, which makes the facility less reliant on fossil fuels. The 1.4L engine facility and the transmission facilities are landfill-free. These facilities use a process to reuse, recycle or convert to energy all waste created in their daily operations, which conserves resources. </p>
<p>  </p>
<p>  Sonic is the only vehicle in its class assembled in the United States. This reduces energy consumption and emissions related to vehicle transport. The Toledo, OH, transmission facility features designated habitat areas certified by the Wildlife Habitat Council, which provide ecological benefits.</p></div>
		</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			End-of-Life Recyclability</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                    After the vehicle’s useful life, 85% of it is recyclable. The majority of its components can be broken down and recycled, which conserves resources and reduces landfill deposits. </p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
</div></div>
